## Ground Truth Analysis

```

```

Since c2 = c6, let me call this value K = 330.2004199209183.

```
= c0*(-c1)*epsilon*T + c0*(c1*K + c3)*epsilon + c5*epsilon**c4*T - c5*K*epsilon**c4
```

So the GT has these terms:
1. `T*epsilon` term: coefficient = c0*(-c1) = 23.788... * (-0.05042...) = -1.19944...
2. `epsilon` term: coefficient = c0*(c1*K + c3) = 23.788...*(0.05042...*330.2... + 1) = 23.788...*(16.645... + 1) = 23.788...*17.645... ≈ 419.78...

4. `epsilon**c4` term: coefficient = -c5*K = -5.2295...*330.2... = -1726.3...

So GT = A*T*epsilon + B*epsilon + C*T*epsilon**p + D*epsilon**p

where p = c4 ≈ 0.9585, and A, B, C, D are specific constants.

This can be rewritten as:
**GT = T*(A*epsilon + C*epsilon^p) + B*epsilon + D*epsilon^p**

The key basis functions are: `T*epsilon`, `epsilon`, `T*epsilon^p`, `epsilon^p` where p ≈ 0.9585.
